zhen ma yin te /
mkhyen gsum gyi steng nas rtogs dgos shing de'i rgyu mtshan yang dbang rnon gyis thog mar mchod brjod kyi tshig thos pa'i tshe /

'phags bzhi bskyed par bstan pas yod ces pa 'di gnyis 'gal lam snyam pa'i dogs pa skye la /
de'i tshe gcig du bral sogs kyi rigs pas dpyad de mkhyen gsum don dam par skye ba med kyang tha snyad tsam du 'phags bzhi skyed bar rtogs pa na sngar gyi dogs pa de sel bar 'gyur gyi /
myu gu bden med rtogs pas mkhyen gsum gyi steng gi dogs pa de sel mi nus pa'i phyir /
der ma zad theg chen dbang rnon gyis sems bskyed kyi sngon du stong nyid rtogs dgos par dbu ma rgyan las gsungs pa lta bu ni thog mar sems kyi chos nyid rtogs dgos te /
de'i rgyu mtshan yang thog mar bden 'dzin spong nus sam mi nus dpyod par 'gyur ba yin la de'ang dri ma sems kyi rang bzhin la ma zhugs pas sems bden med du rtogs pa na bden 'dzin spong nus su mthong ba yin pas skabs don so sor shes par byed dgos gsung /

rtag chad kyi nyen med pas /

nyan thos @# / /
zhes sogs kyi tshig rkang dang pos 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal nye bar zhi ba'i nyer zhi dang /
de sgrub byed kyi thabs dngos su bstan nas ngan song gi sdug bsngal nye bar zhi ba'i nyer zhi btags pa ba dang /
de sgrub byed kyi thabs ring du mi gnas par 'chi ba dran pa dang ngan song gi sdug bsngal bsam pa sogs shugs la bstan pas rkang pa dang pos chung 'bring thun mong gi lam dang /
rkang pa gnyis pas sems bskyed dang /
gsum pas de'i dmigs pa dang bcas pa bstan pas skyes bu chen po'i lam gyi rim pa bstan pa yin gsung /
nyan thos dang de'i phyogs su bstan pa zhes sogs kyi don ni nyan thos zhes pa'i tshig rim pa gcig gis rang rgyal shugs la bstan pa yin la /
'on nyan thos dang khyad par med dam snyam na /
yod de spang bya'i sgo nas gzung rtog spong ba dang /
'bras bu mngon du byed tshul gyi sgo nas srid pa tha ma'i tshe gzhan la ma brten par byang chub 'thob pa /
gzhan don byed tshul gyi sgo nas sgra med lus kyi rnam 'gyur gyis chos ston pa sogs rnam par thar pa cung zad tsam gyis lhag pa yin gsung /
rnam bshad kyi sa bcad ltar na /
yongs su bskor ba de sgrub par byed pa nyid kyis yum de la phyag 'tshal lo / /
zhes pa yan chad kyis mchod brjod bshad thabs lnga'i sgo nas bshad pa de rdzogs pa yin la /
'o na brgal lan gyi gzhung de gang zhe na /
de la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gsum gyis zhes pa nas /
bstod do zhes pa'i bar 'di 'jog cing /
de'ang rtsod pa ni /
rgyan gyi mchod brjod 'di bstan bcos kyi brjod bya dang 'gros mthun pa'i phyag yin zhing /
mngon rtogs thams cad la bstod phyag mdzad 'dod pa yin na mkhyen gsum tsam nyung ba'i skyon dang /
phyogs re tsam la yin na rnam mkhyen gyis kyang chog pas grangs mang ba'i skyon du 'gyur ba'i phyir mi 'thad do zhe na /
lan ni /
mngon rtogs thams cad la yin kyang grangs mang nyung sogs kyi skyon yod pa ma yin te /
mkhyen gsum gyis mngon rtogs mtha' dag nyams len gyi sogs bsdus pa dang /
mkhyen gsum gyis rigs can gsum gyi don thams cad phun sum tshogs par 'gyur bas /
de thugs la bzhag nas mkhyen gsum la bstod phyag mdzad pa yin pa'i phyir zhes pa'o / /
gser phreng ltar na /
de ltar phyag 'tshal pa dang zhes pa nas 'thad pa yin no zhes pa'i bar 'di mchod brjod bshad thabs lnga'i brgal lan gyi gzhung la 'jog dgos la /
rang re'i yig char yang kha cig mchod brjod las 'phros par bsam nas de'i rtsod lan du byed pa ni don cung zad kyang ma rtogs pa'i gtam yin zhes rnam bshad ltar gsungs shing /
de ltar phyag 'tshal ba dang /
bstod pa spon du 'gro bas zhes pa'i tshig 'dis yum de la phyag 'tshal zhes pa yan chad kyis mchod brjod bshad tshar ba'i rnam pa lta bu zhig byas 'dug gsung /
! /
gnyis pa rgyas par phye ste bshad pa la /
dgos don /
bsdus don /
tshig don gsum /
dang po @# / /
la bstan bcos rtsom pa dgos mad kyi dogs pa spangs te brjod bya mkhyen gsum spyi'i rnam gzhag dang /
mdo dang zlos skyon spangs nas dgos pa yod par bsgrub pa gnyis /
dang po ni /
de ltar phyag 'tshal ba /
zhes pa nas /
'thad pa yin no zhes pa'i bar gyi rtsod lan gyi skabs su /
thog mar khong na gnas pa'i dogs pa bsu tshul ni /
bstan bcos kyi brjod bya dang mthun pa'i mchod brjod rtsom pa mkhas pa'i lugs yin pas /
rnam bshad ltar na /
mkhyen gsum la bstod phyag mdzad pa shugs la mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan rtsom par dam bcas pas /
de ltar na yul ston dgos pas gzhi gnyen rnam gsum gang brjod byar bsdus nas rtsom pa yin /
dang po ltar na bstan bcos rtsom pa'i 'bad pa don med pa yin te /
mngon pa nas ma bshad pa bshad rgyu med cing bshad pa ston na rgyun dang mngon pa zlos /
gnyis pa ltar na gnyen po 'ba' zhig ston na rgyan la brten nas slang bya gang gi gnyen po gang yin mi rtogs la /
spang bya dang bcas par ston na nyon mongs sred pa lta bu gcig la'ang bdag rkyen dbang po drug /
dmigs rkyen yul drug /
rgyu rkyen rnam shes drug /
grogs sems byung dang bcas pa ston dgos la /
de la gzhi bstan dgos pas skyon dang po las mi 'da'o / /
gsum pa ltar na rnam pa gzhi med tsam zhig bsdus na skyes bu la mkho ba'i don ma bshad par 'gyur la /
gzhi bsdus na gzhi bsdus pa la bkod pa'i skyon du 'gyur ro zhes rtsod pa 'god do / /
phar phyin rtog ge snang bar /
gzhi gnyen rnam gsum brjod byar byed pa'i bstan bcos rtsom par shes bzhin du re re tsam brjod byar bsdu ba yin nam zhes pa 'dri ba ni 'brel med yin te /
dper na lhas sbyin khyod kyi ming la ci zer zhes 'dri ba dang 'dra bas mi 'thad la /
des na mchod brjod rtsom pas bya ba 'ga' zhig la 'jug par mthong ba na /
khyod kyis bstan bcos shig rtsom par 'dug pas gzhi gnyen rnam gsum gang brjod byar bsdus nas rtsom zhes khong na gnas pa'i dogs pa bsdu bar gsungs pa'i mkhas pa'i bshad tshul mi 'dra la ngo mtshar ba zhig yin gsung /
lan gyi skabs su pha rol po'i shes 'dod ni chos gsum la rmongs pa tsam bzlog pa'i ched du gzhi gnyen rnam gsum re re tsam bsdus pa mi 'thad ces rtsod pa yin pas shes 'dod de gzhir bzhag nas re re tsam ston pa min gyi gsum ka ston pas zlos skyon med ces bshad bya la sbyar te lan ci tsam btab kyang don mthun mi thebs pa ni /
gser phreng las /
de gsum la kha na'i sgra sbyar ba tsam la re bas ni rtsod lan 'di dag bskal ba'i bar du'ang mi shod ces gsungs pa ltar yin gsung /
des na dgos pa dang 'chad tshul mi 'dra ba'i sgo nas lan 'debs tshul ni /
khyod kyi shes 'dod ltar phung khams skye mched kyi rnam grangs dang phan tshun bsdus tshul sogs la rmongs pa bzlog pa'i ched du re re tsam brjod byar bsdus pa de ni ma yin te /
rgyu mtshan gang gi @# / /
phyir na /
yul gzhi gnyen rnam pa gsum char gyis yul can mkhyen gsum mtshon pa'i sgo nas gtan la 'bebs par byed pa'i phyir /
rigs can gsum gyi lam mtha' dag shes par bya ba'i phyir du mkhyen gsum gtan la phab pa la dgos pa yod de /
mkhyen gsum gyis 'phags bzhi'i mngon rtogs mtha' dag bsdus pa'i phyir ro / /
bsdus bar gang las shes she na /
rgyal ba'i yum rnam pa gsum char las zhes shes byed 'god pa yin gsung /
de'ang 'dir mkhyen pa snga ma gnyis rnam gzhag gi rten nyan rang dang byang sems kyi yum du bshad pa'i don /
dper na rgyud dus 'khor gyi grwa tshang lta bu la mtshon na /
de dang de'i grwa pa zhig byed pa la nges par bslab dgos la de las lhag mi dgos pa zhig la de dang de'i thun mong ma yin pa'i 'don cha zer yang /
'don cha de yod pa la grwa tshang de drang de'i grwa pa zhig yin mi dgos pa de bzhin du nyan rang gi nyer zhi tsam don du gnyer bas gzhi shes nges bar dgos la gzhan gnyis mi dgos /
byang sems kyis rigs can gsum gyi don sgrub pas lam shes nges par dgos pas rten gyi gang zag de dang de'i thun mong ma yin pa'i bgo skal lta bur rnam par bzhag kyang /
de gang rung rgyud ldan la rten de gnyis gang rung gis khyab pa yod mi dgos gsung /
de'i phyir zhes pa nas shes pa nyid ces bya'o zhes pa'i bar 'dis mkhyen pa dang po ldan pa la phyi ma gnyis yod dgos pa gcod kyi phyi ma gnyis ldan pa la dang po yod pa mi gcod pa ni /
dper na dge bsnyen gyi spang bya lnga tsam spong ba dang /
bsnyen gnas la spang bya brgyad /
dge tshul la spang bya bcu sogs spong bar bshad pa snga ma snga mas phyi ma phyi ma'i spang bya spong dgos pa gcod kyang phyi mas snga ma'i spang bya spong ba mi gcod pa de bzhin yin gsung /
rnam bshad sogs las rong Tik pas zhing sbyong tshad bshad ba bkag pa la /
de'i slob ma skyed tshal mkhan pos /
'on mi gsal ba'ang gsal ba yin par thal /
sangs rgyas la gsal bar snang ba'i phyir zhes dgag lan mdzad kyang sangs rgyas la mi gsal ba gsal ba yin par ma snang bas dgag pa mi 'gro 'ang rigs pa nyams mtshar ba 'ga' re 'dug ste /
rang re rnams kyis bstan bcos la chos 'khor gyis khyab ces pa la /
'o na 'grel pa don gsal chos can /
mtshan nyid med pa'i chos 'khor yin par thal /
zhes 'phangs pa 'di la chos 'khor gyi don tshang yang mtshan nyid med pa'i chos 'khor gyi don ma tshang zer dgos sam /
sa sde lnga'ang legs phye'i chos 'khor yin par thal /
sogs 'phang na dka' se ba zhig red gsung /
sems can smin tshul du ma yod de /
smin lam zhes pa sbyor lam la byas te /
mdo sde rgyan las /
ji ltar rma dang zas la de dag gi /
zhes sogs ltar sbyor lam gyi tshe zag med kyi chos skye ba la nye bas shing thog smin pa longs spyad rung lta bu dang /
spang bya mthong spang kha bri ba la nye bas rma smin pa brdol ran pa lta bu yin la /
mthong lam skyes pa na zag med kyi @# / /
chos la longs spyod pa'i thog ma dang /
mthong spang spangs pa rang brdol ba la kha btong ba ltar spang bya la kha dod pa yin zhing gos rgyu spun gnyis kyi gcig zad pa dang 'dra bas sgom spang gos hrul lta gyur gsungs pa yin gsung /
de'ang smin pa brgyad yod de /
mdo sde rgyan las /
lus can bral bar smin byed de bzhin du / /
yongs smin rab smin mthun par smin byed gzhan / /
legs par smin byed rtogs par smin byed dang / /
rtag smin gong du smin byed bshad par 'dod / /
ces gsungs pa ltar /
lus can bral bar smin pa ni /
'jig rten pa'i lam gyis mgo mnan pa lta bu ma yin par spang bya'i sa bon dang bral ba ste /
phyogs gcig spang ba mthong lam nas kyang 'jog /
'di'i yongs su zhes pa ma tshang ba med pa ste phyogs re tsam ma yin par sems can ma lus par smin par byed pa yongs smin dang /
phyi rol pa rnams khams 'og ma las chags dral byas te srid rtse'i bar du song yang slar ltung ba'i chos can yin la /
'dir de lta bu ma yin par rab tu smin pa dang /
rang rang gi blo dang 'tsham par chos bstan nas smin pa ni mthun par smin pa dang /
rang don gtso bo dang gzhan don zhar byung lta bu ma yin par gus sbyor dang rtag sbyor gyi brtson 'grus gnyis kyi sgo nas gzhan don gtso bor byed pa'i legs smin dang /
gshegs pa rtogs pa'i don phyir dang / /
zhes pa ltar lam gong ma thob pa la rtogs pa'i sgras bshad pas /
'dir yang rang nyid lam gong mar gshegs nas gzhan der 'god pa ni rtogs par smin pa dang /
res 'ga' tsam ma yin par phyin ci ma log pa'i lam la rtag tu 'khrid par byed pa'i rtag smin dang /
tshogs lam nas sbyor lam de nas mthong sgom lam la rim gyis 'god pa ni gong nas gong du smin par byed pa ste brgyad do / /
rnam pa rtags mtshan ma zhes pa'i me'i ngo bo tsha ba dang dmar lam pa lta bu rnam pa /
'bras bu du ba lta bu rtags rgyu bud shing lta bu mtshan ma la byed de /
rnam thar sgo gsum nang gi mtshan ma med pa'ang rgyu la sbyar nas 'jog dgos pas mtshan ma'i skad dod shes na 'daM la go rgyu zhig yod rgyu red gsung /
mdor bsdus pa las /
nyan thos kyis la slob par 'dod pas kyang sher phyin la bslab par bya zhes pa'i sher phyin ni spyi tsam yin pas /
de'i nang na nyan thos sogs kyis slob rgyu zhig kyang yod pas 'di shes byed du song ba yin gsung /
bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba nyid spang ba can yin no / /
zhes pa 'di la 'khrul nas 'dir bstan yang dag mtha' ngo bo nyid sku yin zer mkhan yang mang po byung gsung /
bstan bcos rtsom pa dgos med kyi rtsod lan 'di slob dpon sogs kyis kha bkang ba yin la /
mdo dang zlos pa'i rtsod lan rje btsun rang gis dngos su gsungs pa yin no /

skye bo blo gros dman pa zhes sogs byung /
'dir dogs pa khong na@# / /

rnam 'grel las /
thugs brtse ldan phyir rtsom kun yang /
gzhan gyi don du sbyor bar byed / /
ces gsungs pa ltar /
ston pa thugs rje can nyid kyis gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa mi mkhyen pa'ang med la mkhyen bzhin du btang snyoms su mdzad pa'ang mi srid pas /
rno 'bring rtul gsum gang gi dbang du byas kyang yum de dang de las dngos brgyad don bdun cu gsal bar mdzad zin pa ma yin nam ste mdzad zin pa'i phyir /
des na gdul bya de gsum gang gi don du'ang rtsom mi dgos zhes pa'i dogs pa khong nas bsus te lan gyi don mdor bsdus na skyon med de /
de dus kyi gdul bya rnams kyi don mdzad zin kyang dus dbang gis de tsam gyis rtogs par mi nus pa'i phyi rabs kyi gdul bya blo dman pa rnams kyi don du rje btsun byams pa dang 'grel byed rnams kyis 'di ltar gsal bar byed pa de sangs rgyas rang nyid kyis mkhyen nas gsal bar ma mdzad pa yin pa dang /
yum gsum gyi sbas don mngon rtogs kyi rim pa rgyan 'dir gang zag gcig 'tshang rgya ba'i nyams len du dril te gsal bar bstan pas bde blag tu rtogs pa'i dgos pa yod ces lan mdzad dgos gsung /
spyir bstan bcos la dgos pa yod pa dang /
de sgrub nus pa dang /
de'ang skye bo mchog gi 'dod bya yin pa dang /
brjod bya 'brel chags pha zhig dgos kyi /
dgos pa med pa bya rog so rtog gi gzhung dang /
sgrub mi nus pa 'jog po'i gtsug rgyan len pa'i gzhung dang /
dam pa'i 'dod bya min pa ma bag mar len pa gzhon nu ba len gyi gzhung /
'brel med pa se'u bcu pa lta bu yin pas de dag mi rung ba'i phyir /
se'u bcu pa ni brjod bya mi 'dra ba bcu bshad pas phal cher drang srong rnams kyis rang gi gsang tshig gzhan gyis shes dogs nas de ltar byas pa yin nam snyam gsung /
ma bag mar len pa'i gzhung ni rig sngags shig yin pa 'dra ste /
bsgrubs nas rdzas la btab ste me la gtor bas me'i nang nas rung zhes pa'i sgra 'byung ba dang /
yang sa cha 'dir mi rung zhes pa'i sgra 'byung ba lta bu zhig yin gsung /
bye smras ming tshig gi spyi zhes pa'i ming ni TIka chen le'u gsum pa ltar sgra spyi dang /

gyis nyams su ma myang ste /
rjod par byed pa yum dang brjod par bya ba theg pa chen po'i lam zab cing rgya che ba dag thabs dang thabs kyis sgrub par bya ba'i tshul gyis 'brel bar mdzad pa'i phyir /
khyab pa yod de /
phyi rol pa theg chen la sdang ba dang /
nyan rang rnams kyis theg chen gyi sde snod sangs rgyas la nyan nas gzhan la sgrogs pa tsam byed kyi /
de dag la dmigs te yun ring por thos bsam sogs mi byed pa'i phyir /
theg pa chen po zhes pa'i che tshul la'ang /
rgyan las /
dmigs pa che ba nyid dang ni / /
zhes sogs ltar dmigs pa che ba sogs bdun dang /
theg bsdus las kyang /
shes bya'i gnas dang mtshan nyid der 'jug dang / /
de yi rgyu 'bras de rab dbye ba dang / /
bslab pa gsum dang de 'bras spangs pa dang / /
ye shes theg pa mchog gyur khyad par 'phags / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar shes bya'i gnas kun gzhi sogs chen po bcu sogs bshad la /
snga ma'i dmigs pa che ba'ang shin tu rgyas pa'i sde snod la dmigs tshul gyi sgo nas yin gsung /
ci la'ang ma reg pa zhes pa gzhan dring mi 'jog pa ste /
de'ang gzhan don byed pa'i tshe gzhan la khags 'gel ba'am /

dbus mtha' las /

zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi chos spyod bcu dang /
rje sa paN gyi bstan pa spyi'i rnam gzhag las yan lag bdun pa'i steng du skyabs 'gro dang smon 'jug gi sems bskyed gnyis dang bcu la chos spyod bcur gsungs pa sogs yod kyang /
'dir ni byang chub kyi sems dang sbyin pa la sogs pa'i sgrub pa'i spyod pa zhes pa 'di la brten nas rnam bshad kyis sems bskyed sogs chos bcu la gsungs pa dang /

rnam bshad ltar na /
byang chub kyi sems zhes pas chos spyod dang po dang /

gser phreng sogs ltar na byang chub kyi sems dang zhes pas spyod pa'i rten sems bskyed dang /
sbyin pa la sogs pa zhes pas spyod pa phar phyin bcu bstan par bzhed gsung /
chos spyod rab gsal zhes pa'i chos spyod de'ang skyabs 'gro nas spyan 'dren khrus gsol sogs mjug bsngo smon shis brjod kyi bar cha tshang ba la zer bas gsol 'debs re re tsam la chos spyod zer ba ni /

zhes pa la /
sa dang por chos can re re'i steng @# / /
du chos nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i rang stobs kyis rang gzhan la bden rlom zhi bas /

sa gnyis par tshul khrims dang /

mchog gi don du rtogs pa sogs mnyam gzhag gi rtogs tshul dang /
rjes thob tu phar phyin lhag tshul la sbyar te phyi ma rnams la'ang 'jog tshul re yod gsung /

gnyis pa bsdus don ni /
de ltar 'brel ba la sogs pa bsnyad nas zhes sogs byung /
'di'i skabs su ma 'dzings pa zhes pa 'a'i 'phul can du 'dug pas 'khrugs mi 'gro ba ste /
de'ang skabs brgyad kyi bstan don dngos po brgyad kyi grangs dang so so'i mtshon byed kyi chos kyi grangs sogs du zhig yod thog mar ma bstan par lu gu rgyud du bshad na /
dngos po brgyad so so'i mgo gang nas tshugs mjug gang du rdzogs pa sogs mi shes par gong 'og 'khrugs par 'gyur bas de sel ba'i phyir dang /
don tshan so so'i sa mtshams sogs ma 'dzings pa'am ma 'khrugs pa'i sgo nas rtogs par bya ba'i phyir du sa bcad ltar thog mar lus mdor bstan gsungs pa yin la /
da'ang shes rab pha rol /

de rnams brgyad / /

nges par 'byung bcas rnams / /

chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa / /

de'ang rten dmigs pa ched du bya ba @# / /

sbyor ba'i khyad par nges 'byed yan lag la gnas pa /
rigs kyi khyad par chos dbyings te /
khyad par bzhi ldan dang /

thar pa don gnyer gyi thar lam cha tshang ba mngon sum du mkhyen pa zhig rnam mkhyen yin no zhes yul gyis yul can mtshon par byed pas skabs dang por lam shes yul gyi ldog cha nas bstan pa dang /

skabs dang po gnyis su lam shes rgyas par dngos su bstan par 'dra'ang ston tshal mi 'dra ba yin gsung /
de'ang lam shes mtshon byed kyi chos bcu gcig yod pas dang po lam shes kyi yan lag la'ang rten gegs nga rgyal mngon gyur dang bral ba sogs lnga yod pa las /
dang po ni /
sangs rgyas kyis sher phyin gyi mdo gsungs pa'i 'khor du rgyal chen ris bzhi sogs 'dod lha rigs drug dang /
tshangs ris pa sogs gzugs khams kyi lha rnams 'dus pa'i tshe de dag rten gegs nga rgyal mngon gyur dang bral te lam shes skye ba'i snod rung du byas pa yin la /
spyir bden pa la gdul bya nyon mongs gang la spyod pa shes nas 'dod chags shas che ba la de'i gnyen po dang /
zhes sdang shas che ba la rdzu 'phrul sogs kyis de'i gnyen por bstan nas zhi bar byas te snod rung du byed pa zhig nges can du dgos pas /
'dir yang lha de dag la rang rang gi thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tan rgyal chen ris bzhi 'jig rten skyong ba'i khur dang /
sum cu rtsa gsum pa longs spyod dang /
'thab bral ba lha ma yin dang 'thab mi dgos par sos bde ba dang /
dga' ldan rnams byams pa bzhugs yod pa dang /
'phrul dga' ba dang /
gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa gnyis rang gi sprul pa dang /
gzhan gyi sprul pa la longs spyod pa sogs kyis nga rgyal skye ba dang /
thams cad la thun mong du yod pa gzugs bzang ba dang /
lus 'od kyi rang bzhin yin pas de dag ngom chos su phyed pa'i mngon pa'i nga rgyal shas che ba yin la /
sangs rgyas kyis lha de dag gi bsam pa mkhyen nas /
gser btso sbyang byas pas lcags g.ya' dag pa zil gyis gnon pa bzhin du /
de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis lha de dag gi 'od zil gyis mnan pas mngon pa'i nga rgyal zhi nas lam shes skye ba'i snod rung du byas gsung /
de'i tshe de dag lam shes dngos skye ba'i snod yin na sbyor lam pa yin dgos pas /
skye ba'i@# / /
gegs de dag dang ldan pa'i nges pa med la sems bskyed gsar du skye ba'i snod la byas na de dag zhi bar byed dgos gsung /
spyir nga rgyal la'ang mngon pa'i nga rgyal sogs du ma yod pas /
yon tan chung du zhig la dmigs nas chen por rlom sems byed pa lta bu mngon pa'i nga rgyal te 'di la yon tan zhig la dmigs pa dgos gsung /
srog gcod dang rku 'phrog byed pa sogs yon tan gtan nas min pa zhig la dmigs te rlom sems byed pa lta bu zhig la log pa'i nga rgyal dang /
rang las mchog tu gyur pa zhig la dmigs te bdag de dang khog cha 'dra'ang 'di 'dra zhig gi cha nas bdag cung zad mi mnyam zhes gnas skabs zhum pa'i rnam pa lta bu zhig yin kyang phal cher mnyam par 'dzin pa'i zhum pa'i nga rgyal dang /
rang las cung zad dma' ba zhig la dmigs te 'di las bdag ches khyad par du 'phags so zhes 'dzin pa lta bu lhag pa'i nga rgyal du 'jog pa sogs yin gsung /
spyir lam shes skye ba dang /
byang chub kyi sems skye ba dang /
chos nyan pa sogs kyi tshe'ang chos la gus pa dang /
mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang bral ba zhig nges can du dgos pas 'dir mtshan gzhi tsam bstan pa dang| chos nyan pa'i kun slong sogs bstan par bla ma snga ma rnams kyis gsungs shing /
nyams len la sbyor shes pa zhig dgos gsung /
chos nyan pa'i tshe de la gus pa dang bkur sti sogs dgos pa ni sngon sangs rgyas kyis mdo zhig gsungs pa'i tshe rgyal po'i btsun mo zhig mi mang po'i nang du 'ong ma nus par g.yog mo zhig btang te sangs rgyas las chos nyan nas /
de shes rab che ba zhig yin pas gang gsungs pa thams cad bzung ste slar 'ong nas btsun mo la gang gsungs thams cad bshad kyang btsun mo de'i rgyud la rtogs pa gang yang ma skyes /
phyi nyin yang g.yog mo de 'ong bas /
btsun mo la 'phrin nas bshad pa de sangs rgyas kyis mkhyen te g.yog mo la /
khyim pas de ltar bshad pa mi chog /
gal te shod zer na sangs rgyas kyis nga'i chos 'di sngon bskal ba mang por dka' ba spyad nas rnyed pa'i chos yin pas ngas kyang bkur sti sogs bya dgos na /
khyod kyis chos la bkur sti sogs med par nyan mi chog bar sangs rgyas kyis smras pa yin zhes btsun mo la shod cig gsungs pas /
des kyang btsun mo la de ltar bshad pas gdan bshams pa sogs chos la bkur sti byas nas nyan pas bden pa mthong ba'i lo rgyus dang /
rgyal po zas gtsang la sems zhum pa dang nga rgyal gnyis yod pas re zhig bar du bden pa mthong ma nus pa yin la /
zhum pa ni gnas skabs der sangs rgyas la lha rnams kyis bsnyen bkur sogs med pas sems zhum pa dang /
rang gi sras sangs rgyas ni rdzu 'phrul sogs che bar mthong nas sems khengs pa yin pas sangs rgyas kyis de'i bsam pa bcos nas thabs mkhas kyis grol bar mdzad pa sogs kyis shes gsung /
sems bskyed rgyud la skyes te thabs @# / /
shes zung 'brel nyams su len pa zhig la lam shes skye yi /

de'ang mdo las /

de dag gi zhes pa /

rtsa bar /

de'ang 'di'i 'grel par /
gnas te rnam pa lnga /
zhes ba tsam las mi 'dug pas gsal kha cher mad kyang gsung lugs la bltas na /

gser 'phreng ltar na /
'gyur 'di la stong pa'i mtshan nyid bdag med pa zhes gcig tu byas te zhi ba'i rnam pa dang bzhir byed dgos shing rtogs dkar de ltar bshad pa 'thad phyogs su mdzad gsung /

dper na /
nad de zas 'dod pa bsten mi chog pha dang /

'di gnyis kyang mi 'dod pa thams cad kyi rtsa ba yin pas /

rma 'bras la byed gsung /

dper na /
'jig rten na gang gnod pa byed pa la dgrar 'dzin pa bzhin no / /

ngan pa dang myur du 'jig pa zhig la de ltar mi phyed pa bzhin du @# / /
'di'ang ngo bo skyon dang bcas pa dang /

yi rang sgom lam ni bla med byang chub tu bsngos pa'i theg chen gyi dge rtsa de gong 'phel du byed pa rjes su yi rang la rag las pas de'i 'og tu yi rang sgom lam 'chad ces mtshams sbyor ba dang /

par yod gsung /
bsam gyis mi khyab tshul ni /

sdug bsngal rtag par med pa'i rnam pa 'di ni /
brgyad stong pa las /

zhes pas bstan la 'dir don dam par ma mchis pa zhes zin byed kyi dbang du byas shing /

mi skye ba zhes pa nyi khri'i tshig @# / /
gi dbang du byas ba yin la /

don gzhan gyi bdag gis dben pa ni /

bshad pas /

rgyu tshogs tshang @# / /
ba'i rgyu 'bras gnyis phan tshun med na mi 'byung ba'i 'brel pa grub par 'dra bas na de ltar bsgrub nus gsung /

yang srid la dga' ba gsum ni rgyu'i rnam pa ste /

'dod na 'jig tshogs lta ba dang /

myur bar gsung ba'ang thud tshon po mar gyi drin zhes zer ba ltar phar phyin theg ba'i lam thun mong bas rgyud sbyangs te tshags su tshud pa na rdo rje theg ba'i bshes gnyen mtshan nyid dang ldan ba las dbang bzhi rdzogs par mnos te bshes gnyen bsten tshul sogs sngar las kyang brgya 'gyur stong 'gyur gyis lhag pa dang /

de ltar na ci phyir gdul bya thams cad la mi snang zhe na /
de dpe'i sgo nas ston pa ni /
lha yi rgyal pos char phab kyang sa bon rul ba sogs mi rung bar gyur pa la myu gu mi 'khrungs pa ltar skal ba med pa la mi snang ngo / /
'dir lha'i rgyal po ni brgya byin la 'dod pa dang /
rgyal chen bzhis rang gi gos rgya mtshor bcug te sprugs nas char 'bebs so zhes gsungs ba sogs yod pa /
gang ltar yang 'jig rten du dge ba byas pas de dag gi stobs sogs 'phel zhing /
des dga' nas 'jig rten la phan pa'i don du char 'bebs so / /
sngar smon gnas mkhyen pa'i skabs su sangs rgyas 'khor ba ji srid bar rtag tu bzhugs par dgag pa dang /

rnam mkhyen de skad cig re re la skye zhing 'jig pa'i phyir dang /
rnal 'byor pa rang rang gis lam sgom stobs kyis rgyud la bzos pas so sor nges pa'i rten gyi rgyud la yod pa'i phyir zhes pa'i rtsod pa khong nas bslangs te /
lan ni 'dus byas kyi mtshan nyid 'jig pa der med pas rtag pa dang /
phyi rol pas lha chen khyab 'jug gis snod bcud thams cad la khyab pas na khyab par bshad pa de lta bu ma yin gyi /
rnam mkhyen gyi rigs 'dra phyi ma 'khor ba ma stongs bar du zad pa'am rgyun chad pa med par gnas pas rtag pa dang /
sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang zag 'di la 'di 'jug 'di la mi 'jug ces mtha' 'dzin mi nus pas na khyab pa zhes brjod pa yin no / /

de la'ang bden 'dzin gyi bag chags drungs nas phyung ba zhig dgos pas /
